)@@G@@ DESIGNS OR TITLES@F@@@@ARE DESIRED, WHILE A BLANK IN COLUMN 11 MEANS THCF
)@@G@@AT A DESIGN IS    @F@@@@WANTED, BUT NO TITLES ARE TO BE PRINTED.  THE LECG
)@@G@@TTER 'T' ENABLES  @A@@@@BOTH THE DESIGN AND TITLE ROUTINES. @[@@@@      CH
)@@G@@@ @@@@  EXAMPLE:     00/00/1972T    @[@@@@      @E@@@@THIS WOULD PRODUCECI

)@@G@@AMPLES ABOVE ARE OPTIONAL.  ANY     @E@@@@         CHARACTER, INCLUDING CL

)@@G@@TERS LONG, TYPED ON SEPARATE CARDS IMMEDIATELY  @E@@@@FOLLOWING THE CALECR
)@@G@@NDAR DATA CARD.  CENTERING OF THE MESSAGE @A@@@@WITHIN THE 30 SPACES IS CS

)@@G@@TIC FEATURE MAY BE OVERRIDDEN BY TWO MORE OPTION LETTERS    @F@@@@PUT INCY

)@@G@@D-G^[DES)DLPETO^[@CTJD1^*[@@@@*SDFF*@E@@@@LOOKEQ IS A FORTRAN SUBROUTINEDI
)@@G@@ ENABLING FORTRAN PROGRAMS TO @G@@@@SEARCH TABLES USING THE HIGH SPPED SDJ
)@@G@@EARCH FUNCTION OF THE UNIVAC 1108.  @D@@@@FOR DETAILS, SEE THE LONG VERSDK
)@@G@@ION OF THIS LISTING.    @[@@@@******@[@@@@      @^@@@@THE LOOKEQ CALL ISDL
)@@G@@:     @[@@@@      @A@@@@         I=LOOKEQ(ARG,TAB,LEN,MASK) @[@@@@      DM
)@@G@@@F@@@@     ARG IS THE ITEM BEING SEARCHED FOR, E.G. IF YOU ARE SEARCHINGDN
)@@G@@@F@@@@ FOR THE FIRST OCCURENCE OF THE NUMBER 3.25279841, THEN YOU WOULD DO
)@@G@@@ @@@@ SET ARG EQUAL TO 3.25279841. @B@@@@     TAB IS THE TABLE TO BE SEDP
)@@G@@ARCHED.     @A@@@@     LEN IS THE LENGTH OF THE TABLE.@F@@@@     I WILL DQ
)@@G@@BE SET EQUAL TO THE INDEX INTO THE TABLE WHERE THE    @F@@@@ CONTENTS OFDR
)@@G@@ ARG WERE FOUND. IF THERE WAS NO FIND, I WILL BE SET  @]@@@@ TO ZERO.   DS
)@@G@@@F@@@@     MASK, IF SET NONZERO, WILL CAUSE THE SEARCH TO BE A MASKED   DT
)@@G@@@F@@@@ SEARCH. THAT IS, IF THE MASK HAS THE VALUE 077770000 OCTAL, THE  DU
)@@G@@@E@@@@ SEARCH WILL CONSIDER ONLY THE MIDDLE THIRD OF EACH WORD.   @[@@@@DV
)@@G@@      @]@@@@ EXAMPLE:   @[@@@@      @ @@@@         DIMENSION LIST(35)   DW
)@@G@@@ @@@@         LIST(12)='KEPOOT'    @C@@@@         I=LOOKEQ('CAHOOT',LISDX
)@@G@@T,35,0777777)     @[@@@@      @F@@@@     THIS WILL SEARCH THE 35 WORDS ODY
)@@G@@F THE ARRAY LIST, LOOKING FOR @F@@@@ THR FIRST WORD WHOSE BOTTOM HALF ISDZ
)@@G@@ THE SAME AS THE BOTTOM HALF  @F@@@@ OF 'CAHOOT'. IT WILL RETURN A VALUEEA
)@@G@@ 12, BECAUSE THE BOTTOM HALF  @F@@@@ OF LIST(12)='OOT', THE SAME AS THE EB
)@@G@@BOTTOM HALF OF THE ARGUMENT.  @[@@@@      @]@@@@ NOTES:     @[@@@@      EC
)@@G@@@E@@@@     THE RESULT WILL BE MOST USEFUL IF THE TABLE IS A ONE-  @F@@@@ED
)@@G@@ DIMENSIONED ARRAY, BECAUSE IN THAT CASE THE VALUE OF I MAY BE    @^@@@@EE
)@@G@@ USED AS A SUBSCRIPT.   @D@@@@     IF MASKING IS NOT DESIRED, SPECIFY O EF
)@@G@@AS THE MASK.@F@@@@     USERS OF THE @MAD COMPILER WILL NOT NEED THIS ROUEG
)@@G@@TINE, BUT   @F@@@@ MAY INSTEAD USE THE .FIND. AND .SEARCH. FUNCTIONS OF EH
)@@G@@THE MAD     @]@@@@ COMPILER.  ___ET ^[OD[ ^[]D9OE-JD*)D[[D-A@K@@@@^[JC0)EI

)@@G@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@*[@@@@*SDFF*@E@@@@C     GBILL - CATALOGUED FILE EV
)@@G@@INFORMATION BY ACCOUNT NUMBER @[@@@@      @ @@@@      COMPILER (DATA=IBMEW
)@@G@@)     @^@@@@      EXTERNAL ERROR    @ @@@@      IMPLICIT INTEGER (A-Z)  EX
)@@G@@@G@@@@      PARAMETER AX = 500 @ IF CHANGED, MUST BE CHANGED IN DRECGT AEY
)@@G@@S WELL@B@@@@      LOGICAL UNTIL,SETC,CARE,FLAG,LONG   @G@@@@      DIMENSEZ
)@@G@@ION ACNOS(1000),F4(AX),F2(AX),F17(AX),F14(AX),F40(AX),VOP(A @G@@@@     *FA
)@@G@@X),SEC(AX),REM(AX),SUM(8,5),ACCT(4),NFILES(AX),LABEL(4,8),GOP(AX) @G@@@@FB
)@@G@@      COMMON /A/DATE,TIME,OPTION,UNTIL/B/ACNOS,NFILES,VOP,GOP,F2,F4,F17,FC
)@@G@@@F@@@@     *F14,F40,REM,SEC,ACX,PROJ1,PROJ2,QUAL1,QUAL2,UNLTOT/C/ACCT   FD
)@@G@@@H@@@@      DATA LONG/.FALSE./FLAG/.FALSE./,PRINTD/0/,UNTIL/.TRUE./  @ AFE
)@@G@@SSUME DEMAND@D@@@@      DATA LABEL(1,1)/'IN HOUSE                '/     FF

)@@G@@ORED RESEARCH    '/     @D@@@@      DATA LABEL(1,6)/'STUDENT (T,U,G) ACCFJ
)@@G@@TS   '/     @D@@@@      DATA LABEL(1,7)/'EXEC                    '/     FK
)@@G@@@D@@@@      DATA LABEL(1,8)/'OTHER                   '/     @[@@@@      FL
)@@G@@@[@@@@      @[@@@@      @A@@@@      DEFINE X(Y) = FLD(Y,1,OPTION) @#@@@@FM
)@@G@@      PROJ1 = 0   @#@@@@      PROJ2 = 0   @#@@@@      QUAL1 = 0   @#@@@@FN
)@@G@@      QUAL2 = 0   @C@@@@      CALL GETR(ITYPE)   @ GET OPTIONS, RUN TYPEFO
)@@G@@@[@@@@      @A@@@@C     CHECK FOR L AND N OPTIONS     @[@@@@      @B@@@@FP
)@@G@@      IF (X(21) .EQ. 1) LONG = .TRUE.     @#@@@@      X(21) = 0   @A@@@@FQ
)@@G@@      IF (X(23) .EQ. 1) CALL DIREND @#@@@@      X(23) = 0   @F@@@@      FR
)@@G@@IF (OPTION .EQ. 0) X(10) = 1  @ IF NO OPTIONS, SET A-OPTION @F@@@@      FS
)@@G@@IF (OPTION.EQ.5.AND.ITYPE.EQ.7.AND..NOT.UNTIL) SETC = .TRUE.@B@@@@      FT
)@@G@@PRINT 1000, DATE, TIME   @ SIGN ON  @F@@@@      IF (UNTIL .AND. .NOT. LOFU
)@@G@@NG) PRINT 1001  @ SHORT HEADING     @E@@@@      IF (.NOT. UNTIL .OR. LONFV
)@@G@@G) PRINT 1002   @ LONG HEADING@E@@@@      CALL DIRINT(ERROR,ACCT,4,0)   FW
)@@G@@@ CALL DIREC$ FOR MFD   @G@@@@      IF(X(10).EQ.0.AND.X(25).EQ.0.AND.X(2FX
)@@G@@6).EQ.0.AND.X(15).EQ.0)GOTO220@B@@@@      CALL SINF       @ PICK UP SPECFY
)@@G@@ FIELD@E@@@@      IF (X(10) .EQ. 1) GO TO 220     @ A-OPTION (ACCOUNT)  FZ
)@@G@@@E@@@@      IF (X(15) .EQ. 1) GO TO 219     @ F-OPTION (FILE)     @^@@@@GA
)@@G@@      QUAL1 = ACCT(1)   @#@@@@      ACCT(1) = 0 @^@@@@      QUAL2 = ACCTGB
)@@G@@(2)   @#@@@@      ACCT(2) = 0 @E@@@@      IF (X(26) .EQ. 1) GO TO 220   GC
)@@G@@  @ Q-OPTION (QUALIFIER)@^@@@@      PROJ1 = QUAL1     @#@@@@      QUAL1 GD
)@@G@@= 0   @^@@@@      PROJ2 = QUAL2     @#@@@@      QUAL2 = 0   @#@@@@      GE
)@@G@@GO TO 220   @^@@@@219   QUAL1 = ACCT(1)   @^@@@@      QUAL2 = ACCT(2)   GF
)@@G@@@^@@@@      PROJ1 = ACCT(3)   @^@@@@      PROJ2 = ACCT(4)   @C@@@@220   GG
)@@G@@CALL DRECGT        @ SEARCH THE DIRECTORY @F@@@@      IF (X(33).EQ.0.OR.GH
)@@G@@X(34).EQ.1.OR.X(35).EQ.0) CARE = .TRUE.   @G@@@@      IF((X(15).EQ.1.OR.GI
)@@G@@X(25).EQ.1.OR.X(26).EQ.1).AND.X(10).EQ.0)CARE=  @#@@@@     * .FALSE.    GJ
)@@G@@@D@@@@   17 DO 100 I = 1,ACX     @ FOR EACH ACCOUNT FOUND   @#@@@@      GK
)@@G@@II = I*2 - 1@D@@@@      A = FLD(0,6,ACNOS(II))     @ GET FIRST CHAR     GL
)@@G@@@D@@@@      B = FLD(0,24,ACNOS(II))    @ GET FIRST 4 CHARS  @ @@@@      GM
)@@G@@IF (.NOT.CARE) GO TO 10 @D@@@@      IF (X(10) .EQ. 0) GO TO 18       @ AGN
)@@G@@-OPTION?    @G@@@@      IF (ACNOS(II).NE.ACCT(1).OR.ACNOS(II+1).NE.ACCT(GO
)@@G@@2)) GO TO 100     @^@@@@      FLAG = .TRUE.     @#@@@@      GO TO 10    GP
)@@G@@@E@@@@   18 IF (X(12) .EQ. 1) GO TO 30  @ C-OPTION (ROCKEFELLER)  @D@@@@GQ
)@@G@@      IF (X(14) .EQ. 1) GO TO 85  @ E-OPTION (EXEC)   @E@@@@      IF (X(GR
)@@G@@17) .EQ. 1) GO TO 10  @ H-OPTION (IN-HOUSE)     @D@@@@      IF (X(18) .EGS
)@@G@@Q. 1) GO TO 80  @ I-OPTION (OTHER)  @E@@@@      IF (X(20) .EQ. 1) GO TO GT
)@@G@@60  @ K-OPTION (STUDENTS)     @E@@@@      IF (X(22) .EQ. 1) GO TO 20  @ GU
)@@G@@M-OPTION (MED CENTER)   @F@@@@      IF (X(24) .EQ. 1) GO TO 40  @ O-OPTIGV
)@@G@@ON (SPONSORED RESEARCH) @G@@@@      IF (X(27) .EQ. 1) GO TO 50  @ R-OPTIGW
)@@G@@ON (UNSPONSORED RESEARCH)     @B@@@@      GO TO 100        @ NONE OF THEGX
)@@G@@ ABOVE@C@@@@   10 IF (ACNOS(II) .NE. '0-0040') GO TO 110    @^@@@@      GY
)@@G@@FLAG = .TRUE.     @B@@@@      SUM(1,5) = SUM(1,5) + NFILES(I)     @G@@@@GZ
)@@G@@      SUM(1,1) = SUM(1,1) + F2(I) + F4(I) + F17(I) + F14(I) + F40(I)    HA
)@@G@@@A@@@@      SUM(1,2) = SUM(1,2) + REM(I)  @C@@@@      SUM(1,3) = SUM(1,3HB
)@@G@@) + VOP(I) + GOP(I)     @A@@@@      SUM(1,4) = SUM(1,4) + SEC(I)  @ @@@@HC
)@@G@@  110 IF (X(17).EQ.1)GO TO 80 @ @@@@   20 IF (A .NE. 56) GO TO 120@^@@@@HD
)@@G@@      FLAG = .TRUE.     @G@@@@      SUM(2,1) = SUM(2,1) + F2(I) + F4(I) HE
)@@G@@+ F17(I) + F14(I) + F40(I)    @B@@@@      SUM(2,5) = SUM(2,5) + NFILES(IHF

)@@G@@@^@@@@      FLAG = .TRUE.     @G@@@@      SUM(3,1) = SUM(3,1) + F2(I) + HJ

)@@G@@ILES(I)     @A@@@@      SUM(3,2) = SUM(3,2) + REM(I)  @C@@@@      SUM(3,HL
)@@G@@3) = SUM(3,3) + VOP(I) + GOP(I)     @A@@@@      SUM(3,4) = SUM(3,4) + SEHM
)@@G@@C(I)  @ @@@@  130 IF (X(12).EQ.1)GO TO 80 @A@@@@   40 IF (B .NE. 6H@@0-5HN
)@@G@@5) GO TO 140@^@@@@      FLAG = .TRUE.     @G@@@@      SUM(4,1) = SUM(4,1HO
)@@G@@) + F2(I) + F4(I) + F17(I) + F14(I) + F40(I)    @B@@@@      SUM(4,5) = SHP
)@@G@@UM(4,5) + NFILES(I)     @A@@@@      SUM(4,2) = SUM(4,2) + REM(I)  @C@@@@HQ
)@@G@@      SUM(4,3) = SUM(4,3) + VOP(I) + GOP(I)     @A@@@@      SUM(4,4) = SHR
)@@G@@UM(4,4) + SEC(I)  @ @@@@  140 IF (X(24).EQ.1)GO TO 80 @A@@@@   50 IF (B.HS
)@@G@@ NE. 6H@@0-05) GO TO 150@^@@@@      FLAG = .TRUE.     @G@@@@      SUM(5,HT
)@@G@@1) = SUM(5,1) + F2(I) + F4(I) + F17(I) + F14(I) + F40(I)    @B@@@@      HU
)@@G@@SUM(5,5) = SUM(5,5) + NFILES(I)     @A@@@@      SUM(5,2) = SUM(5,2) + REHV
)@@G@@M(I)  @C@@@@      SUM(5,3) = SUM(5,3) + VOP(I) + GOP(I)     @A@@@@      HW
)@@G@@SUM(5,4) = SUM(5,4) + SEC(I)  @ @@@@  150 IF (X(27).EQ.1)GO TO 80 @F@@@@HX
)@@G@@   60 IF (A .NE. 25 .AND. A .NE. 26 .AND. A .NE. 12) GO TO 160    @^@@@@HY

)@@G@@*[@@@@*SDFF*@D@@@@GBILL IS THE MASS STORAGE BILLING PROCESSOR.  FOR MOREPG
)@@G@@@C@@@@INFORMATION, SEE THE LONG VERSION OF THIS ITEM. @[@@@@******@[@@@@PH
)@@G@@      @F@@@@    THE GBILL PROCESSOR IS USED BY UHMC TO DETERMINE THE AMOPI
)@@G@@UNT   @F@@@@OF MASS STORAGE BEING USED BY EACH ACCOUNT, AND TO COMPUTE BPJ
)@@G@@ILLS  @F@@@@ACCORDINGLY.  IT IS NOW AVAILABLE TO THE USER, WHO MAY USE IPK
)@@G@@T TO  @F@@@@DETERMINE WHAT HE IS BEING BILLED FOR, HOW MUCH MASS STORAGEPL
)@@G@@ HE   @E@@@@IS USING, OR WHAT DEVICES HIS FILES ARE ON.  THE CALL IS:   PM
)@@G@@@[@@@@      @A@@@@       @GBILL<,OPTIONS>   <SPEC>    @[@@@@      @A@@@@PN
)@@G@@WHERE THE RECOGNIZED OPTIONS ARE:   @[@@@@      @A@@@@       A - SPEC ISPO
)@@G@@ AN ACCOUNT NUMBER@ @@@@       F - SPEC IS A FILENAME @D@@@@       L - LPP
)@@G@@ONG LISTING (SHORT IS ASSUMED IF TTY)     @A@@@@       P - SPEC IS A PROPQ
)@@G@@JECT-ID     @G@@@@           (MUST BE PRIVILEGED TO ACCESS PROJ-ID'S OTHPR
)@@G@@ER THAN YOUR OWN) @ @@@@       Q - SPEC IS A QUALIFIER@[@@@@      @E@@@@PS
)@@G@@IF NO OPTIONS ARE SPECIFIED, 'A' IS ASSUMED, AND THE USER'S @^@@@@ACCOUNPT
)@@G@@T NUMBER IS USED. @[@@@@      @ @@@@TO DETERMINE THE MASS STORAGE @F@@@@PU
)@@G@@USAGE FOR YOUR ACCOUNT: @GBILL,A ACCOUNT  -OR-  TO DETERMINE MASS @E@@@@PV
)@@G@@STORAGE USAGE OF A PARTICULAR FILE: @GBILL,F QUAL*FILE.     @[@@@@      PW
)@@G@@@E@@@@GBILL'S PRINTED OUTPUT (SHORT FOR DEMAND) HAS COLUMNS WITH  @^@@@@PX
)@@G@@THE FOLLOWING TOTALS:   @[@@@@      @^@@@@       NUMBER OF FILES  @ @@@@PY
)@@G@@       TOTAL FIXED TRACKS     @^@@@@       REMOVABLE TRACKS @A@@@@      PZ
)@@G@@ SECURE BACKUP TAPE BLOCKS    @^@@@@       V-OPTION TRACKS  @^@@@@      QA
)@@G@@ G-OPTION TRACKS  @#@@@@       F2 TRACKS  @#@@@@       F4 TRACKS  @#@@@@QB
)@@G@@       F17 TRACKS @^@@@@       F14 FIXED TRACKS @^@@@@       F40 FIXED TQC
)@@G@@RACKS @[@@@@      @F@@@@IF MORE THAN ONE ACCOUNT IS LISTED, A SUMMARY TOQD
)@@G@@TAL FOR ALL THE   @B@@@@ACCOUNTS LISTED WILL BE PRINTED, AS WELL. ___ 0)QE

)@@G@@      . WERE ANY SUBSTITUTES GIVEN? @D@@@@          J         RETN      VO
)@@G@@            . NO, RETURN@C@@@@          L         A1,X1                 VP
)@@G@@.     @E@@@@          LSSL      A1,1                  . DOUBLE THE INDEXVQ
)@@G@@@E@@@@          S         A1,X2                 . AND STORE IN X2 @E@@@@VR
)@@G@@          DSL       A1,72                 . ZERO OUT A1, A2 @]@@@@EACH  VS
)@@G@@.     @E@@@@          DL        A4,MASK0              . GET ALL 7'S     VT
)@@G@@@E@@@@          DS        A4,ACMASK             . STORE IN ACMASK @F@@@@VU
)@@G@@          LR,U      R3,11                 . SET UP FOR 12 CHARS   @G@@@@VV
)@@G@@          SZ        A0                    . OK  BOYS, FROM THE TOP!     VW
)@@G@@@F@@@@PARACT    EX        ACLD,A0               . GET A CHAR OF CKACT,A2VX
)@@G@@@D@@@@          TNE,U     A4,047                . IS IT A $ @H@@@@      VY
)@@G@@    EX        ACST,A0               . YES, SZ IN THAT PART OF ACMASK    VZ
)@@G@@@F@@@@          AA,U      A0,1                  . GET SET FOR NEXT CHAR WA
)@@G@@@D@@@@          JGD       R3,PARACT             . DO 12     @F@@@@      WB
)@@G@@    DL        A4,CKACT,A2           . GET FULL CHECK-ACCT   @G@@@@      WC
)@@G@@    AND       A5,ACMASK+1           . MASK OUT TRANS ($) CHARS    @C@@@@WD
)@@G@@          AND       A4,ACMASK             .     @F@@@@          DS      WE
)@@G@@  A5,HOLDAC             . STORE RESULT IN HOLDAC@F@@@@          DL      WF
)@@G@@  A4,ACCT,X2            . GET REAL FULL ACCT    @G@@@@          AND     WG
)@@G@@  A5,ACMASK+1           . AND DO THE SAME THING TO IT @C@@@@          ANWH
)@@G@@D       A4,ACMASK             .     @G@@@@          DTE       A5,HOLDAC WI
)@@G@@            . IS RESULT SAME AS HOLDAC?   @F@@@@          J         NEXTWJ
)@@G@@                  . NO, TRY NEXT CKACT    @F@@@@          L         A4,CWK
)@@G@@KNO               . YES, GET MATCHING CKNO@F@@@@          S         A4,NWL
)@@G@@YUNO              . AND STORE IN NYUNO(I) @F@@@@NEXT      AA,U      A1,1WM
)@@G@@                  . GET SET FOR NEXT CKACT@C@@@@          AA,U      A2,2WN
)@@G@@                  .     @E@@@@          TLE       A1,MM                 WO
)@@G@@. FINISHED YET?   @F@@@@          J         EACH                  . NO, WP
)@@G@@CHECK NEXT CKACT  @ @@@@RETN      L         X1,STORE  @ @@@@          L WQ
)@@G@@        X2,STORE+1@ @@@@          J         2,X11     @[@@@@$(2)  @A@@@@WR
)@@G@@A         INFO      2         2     @E@@@@AX        EQU       200       WS
)@@G@@            . MAX ACCOUNTS    @F@@@@CKACT     RES       AX*2            WT
)@@G@@      . PARTIAL ACCOUNT ARRARY@F@@@@ACCT      RES       AX*2            WU
)@@G@@      . UHMC ACCOUNT ARRAY    @G@@@@NO        RES       AX              WV
)@@G@@      . LINK TO NYUACT FOR EACH ACCT@H@@@@MM        RES       1         WW
)@@G@@            . NO. OF PARTIAL ACCOUNTS TO CHECK  @ @@@@CKNO      EQUF    WX
)@@G@@  NO,A1,H1  @ @@@@NYUNO     EQUF      NO,X1,H2  @#@@@@          END     WY
)@@G@@___     MM                    . WERE ANY SUBSTITUTES GIVEN? @D@@@@      WZ
)@@G@@MI1         MI0         DIRSEC      REVT        REVO        REVG        XA
)@@G@@POLTRAN     GOTONE      DIRECERR    DOSORT      QF900       REVV        XB
)@@G@@DIRLNK      ACMASK      MFD$        PCT         RPRL        REVR        XC
)@@G@@DATREF      REVD        SZOPT       SZLOD       SZBAK       UNCHEK      XD

)@@G@@CHK000      @@[@@@@@@@@@GALI        @@[@@@@@@@@4LNKRTN      @@[@@@@@@@[>XG
